{{Evento futuro}}
Essa é uma linha do tempo para '''todas as mídias [[Cânon|canônicas]] de ''[[Star Wars]]''''' lançadas, incluindo filmes, livros, quadrinhos, curtas, material promocional, séries de TV e jogos.

|data-sort-value=-19 |c. [[19 ABY]]<ref name="Chaos Rising">Os eventos de ''[[Thrawn: Alliances]]'' que ocorrem durante as [[Guerras Clônicas]] acontecem depois do [[Julgamento de Ahsoka Tano|julgamento e expulsão]] de [[Ahsoka Tano]]. ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' posiciona ambos no final das Guerras Clônicas em [[19 ABY]]. Como alguns eventos de ''[[Thrawn Ascendancy: Chaos Rising]]'' acontecem ao mesmo tempo que esses de ''[[Thrawn: Alliances]]'', eles devem ocorrer no mesmo [[Ano padrão|ano]] de 19 ABY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #8DB3E2; text-align: center;" | R ||''[[Thrawn Ascendancy: Chaos Rising]]'' †

|data-sort-value=-18 |c. [[18 ABY]]<ref name="Greater Good">Os eventos de ''[[Thrawn: Alliances]]'' que ocorrem durante as [[Guerras Clônicas]] acontecem depois do [[Julgamento de Ahsoka Tano|julgamento e expulsão]] de [[Ahsoka Tano]]. ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' posiciona ambos no final das Guerras Clônicas em [[19 ABY]]. Como alguns eventos de ''[[Thrawn Ascendancy: Chaos Rising]]'' acontecem ao mesmo tempo que esses de ''[[Thrawn: Alliances]]'', eles devem ocorrer no mesmo [[Ano padrão|ano]] de 19 ABY. Além disso, ''Thrawn [[Ascendancy: Greater Good]]'' estabelece que o [[ataque na Paataatus]], que havia sido mostrado em ''Chaos Rising'', ocorreu um ano antes. Portanto, os eventos de ''Greater Good'' devem ocorrer por volta de [[18 ABY]].</ref> ||style="background-color: #8DB3E2; text-align: center;" | R ||''[[Thrawn Ascendancy: Greater Good]]'' †

|data-sort-value=-14 |[[14 ABY]]<ref name="DV18 date">{{DVDLotS18}}</ref> ||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | Q ||[[Darth Vader (2017) 18|''Darth Vader'' (2017) 18]]
||[[Charles Soule]]
|| 11/07/2018
|- class="comic"
|[[14 ABY]]<ref name="DV 19/20/21/22">The events of [[Tarkin (romance)|''Tarkin'']] take place five [[Standard year|years]] after the [[Proclamation of the New Order|rise]] of the [[Galactic Empire]], which ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' dates to [[19 ABY]]. Therefore, ''Tarkin'' must be set in [[14 ABY]]. As [[Anakin Skywalker|Darth Vader]] knows about [[Wilhuff Tarkin]]'s past on [[Eriadu]] in [[Darth Vader (2017) 18|''Darth Vader'' (2017) 18]], which he only learned about in ''Tarkin'', issue 18 must take place after the novel. The later issue [[Darth Vader (2017) 19|''Darth Vader'' (2017) 19]] featured the [[Second Sister]], who was [[Death|killed]] in ''[[Star Wars Jedi: Fallen Order]]''. ''Fallen Order'' takes place five years after the [[Great Jedi Purge]], which is dated to 19 BBY by ''Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico''. Therefore, ''Star Wars Jedi: Fallen Order'' is also set in 14 BBY. As ''Darth Vader: Dark Lord of the Sith 19'' is set immediately after issue 18, and issues 20, 21 and 22 all take place after each other, it means that all these issues take place in [[14 ABY]].</ref> ||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | Q ||[[Darth Vader (2017) 19|''Darth Vader'' (2017) 19]]
||[[Charles Soule]]

|data-sort-value=-10 |[[10 ABY]]<ref name="Timelines" /> ||style="background-color: #92CDDC; text-align: center;" | F ||''[[Han Solo: Uma História Star Wars]]''
*<small>Prelúdio ocorre em [[13 ABY]].<ref name="Solo prologue">''[[Solo: A Star Wars Story The Official Guide]]'' establishes that the events of ''Solo: A Star Wars Story'' begin nine [[Standard year|years]] after the [[Proclamation of the New Order|founding]] of the [[Galactic Empire]]. ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' dates the Empire's founding to [[19 ABY]], meaning the events of ''Solo'' can be placed in [[10 ABY]]. Because the prologue takes place three years prior, the prologue must take place in [[13 ABY]].</ref></small>

|c. [[4 ABY|4]]&ndash;[[3 ABY]]<ref name="DisarmingLesson">"A Disarming Lesson" acontece depois que [[Ezra Bridger]] conhece [[Ahsoka Tano]] em "[[Fire Across the Galaxy]]," mas antes de [[Sabre de luz de Ezra Bridger|seu sabre de luz]] ser destruído em "[[Twilight of the Apprentice]]." ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' posiciona "Fire Across the Galaxy" em [[4 ABY]], e, de acordo com ''[[Star Wars: Absolutely Everything You Need to Know, Updated and Expanded]]'', [[Ahsoka Tano]] tinha 14 [[Ano padrão|anos]] quando [[Sexos|ela]] se tornou [[Padawan]] de [[Anakin Skywalker]] e 32 quando ela lutou contra Darth Vader em "Twilight of the Apprentice." ''Star Wars: Galactic Atlas'' diz que Tano se tornou aprendiz de Skywalker em [[22 ABY]], o que significa que "Twilight of the Apprentice" não pode acontecer depois de [[3 ABY]]. ''[[Dawn of Rebellion]]'' posiciona "[[The Mystery of Chopper Base]]" em 3 ABY, e, já que "Twilight of the Apprentice" acontece depois desse episódio, ele deve acontecer também em 3 ABY. Portanto, "A Disarming Lesson" acontece entre 4 ABY e 3 ABY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #B7DDE8; text-align: center;" | TV ||[[A Disarming Lesson|''Forces of Destiny'': Temporada 2: Episódio 15: "A Disarming Lesson"]] †
||[[Nicole Dubuc]]

|data-sort-value=-4 |Between [[4 ABY]] and [[3 ABY]]<ref name="Heist">''[[Star Wars Rebels: Imperial Heist]]'' includes [[Sabine Wren]] with [[Color|blue-green]] [[hair]], which first appears in "[[The Lost Commanders]]," however it takes place before [[Kanan Jarrus]] was blinded in "[[Twilight of the Apprentice]]." ''[[Star Wars: The Clone Wars: Character Encyclopedia - Join the Battle!]]'' states that [[Rex]] was [[Reproduction|born]] thirty-two [[Standard year|years]] before the events of {{Filme|IV}}, which ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' places in [[0 ABY]]. Therefore, Rex must have been born in [[32 ABY]]. As it also states that Rex is 28 during "The Lost Commanders", this episode must take place in [[4 ABY]]. As {{SW|url=news/swca-2022-lucasfilm-publishing-behind-the-page-panel|text=SWCC 2022: 7 Things We Learned from the Lucasfilm Publishing Behind the Page Panel}}, dates "Twilight of the Apprentice" to [[3 ABY]], ''Star Wars Rebels: Imperial Heist'' must take place between these years.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C3D69B; text-align: center;" | J ||''[[Star Wars Rebels: Imperial Heist]]'' †

|data-sort-value=-3 |c. [[4 ABY|4]]&ndash;[[2 ABY]]<ref name="SecondChance">[[Sabine Wren]] aparece em "The Second Chance" com seu [[cabelo]] [[Cor|azul e verde]], que é mostrado pela primeira vez em "[[The Lost Commanders]]". Além disso, o seu cabelo é roxo e branco em ''[[Star Wars Rebels: Steps Into Shadow]]'', o que significa que "The Second Chance" deve acontecer algum tempo antes. ''[[Star Wars: Timelines]]'' posiciona "The Lost Commanders" e ''Star Wars Rebels: Steps Into Shadow'' em [[4 ABY]] and [[2 ABY]] respectivamente, o que resulta em "The Second Chance" sendo datado entre esses anos.</ref> ||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | Q ||"[[The Second Chance]]"

|- class="videogame"
|data-sort-value=-2 |c. [[2 ABY]]&ndash;[[1 ABY]]<ref name="Special Ops">''Special Ops'' features [[Sabine Wren]] with light [[color|purple]] [[hair]] and a [[jetpack]], placing it after the events of ''[[Imperial Supercommandos]]'', where she obtains the jetpack, and before ''[[The Occupation]]'', where her hair is deep purple. ''[[Dawn of Rebellion]]'' dates the events of ''[[Star Wars Rebels: Steps Into Shadow]]'' seventeen [[Standard year|years]] after the end of the [[Clone Wars]], which ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' dates to [[19 ABY]]; therefore, the events of ''Steps Into Shadow'' must take place in [[2 ABY]] and ''Imperial Supercommandos'', which comes after, can be set no earlier than [[2 ABY]]. Because Sabine Wren's hair is deep purple in "[[The Occupation]]", ''Special Ops'' must take place prior to that episode. The trivia guide for ''[[Star Wars Rebels: Heroes of Mandalore]]'' states that [[Bo-Katan Kryze]] was redesigned to advance the character's age by "18 [[Standard year|years]] or so". As she was last seen was in "[[The Lawless]]", which ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' places in [[19 ABY]], it can be assumed that the events of ''Heroes of Mandalore'', as well as ''The Occupation'' take place in approximately 1 BBY. Because Special Ops must be set between these episodes, this information places it between 2 BBY and 1 BBY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C3D69B; text-align: center;" | J ||''[[Star Wars Rebels: Special Ops]]'' †

|c. [[3 ABY|3]]&ndash;[[0 ABY]]<ref name="Beast Within">A "The Beast Within" apresenta o [[segundo sabre de luz de Ezra Bridger]], que foi construído depois dos eventos de "[[Twilight of the Apprentice]]." De acordo com {{SW|url=news/swca-2022-lucasfilm-publishing-behind-the-page-panel|text=SWCC 2022: 7 Things We Learned from the Lucasfilm Publishing Behind the Page Panel}}, "Twilight of the Apprentice" acontece em [[3 ABY]]. Além disso, [[Ezra Bridger]] desaparece durante os eventos de "[[Family Reunion – and Farewell]]", que, de acordo com ''[[The Star Wars Book]]'', acontece no mesmo [[Ano padrão|ano]] da [[Batalha de Yavin]], ou seja, [[0 ABY]]. Portanto, "The Beast Within" acontece algum tempo entre 3 ABY e 0 ABY.</ref>||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | Q ||"[[The Beast Within]]" †

|- class="short"
|data-sort-value=0 |Between [[2 ABY]] and [[0 ABY]]<ref name="Inbrief Date">''[[Star Wars: On the Front Lines]]'' places the [[Declaration of the Rebel Alliance]] two [[Standard year|years]] before the [[Battle of Yavin]], or [[2 ABY]]. As the Rebel Alliance appears in "Inbrief," it must therefore have taken place during or after 2 [[Galactic calendar|BBY]]. Furthermore, in ''[[Battlefront: Companhia do Crepúsculo]]'', the [[rebel trooper]] [[Hazram Namir]] refers to [[Brand]] as a [[bounty hunter]] during the [[battle on Vir Aphshire]], which occurs concurrently with the [[Battle of Yavin]]. As Brand's [[bounty]] [[Hunting|hunter]] past was not known by other rebels until the events of "Inbrief", it must take place prior to the Battle of [[Yavin Prime|Yavin]], or [[0 ABY]]. Therefore "Inbrief" takes place in between 2 BBY and 0 BBY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C6D9F0; text-align: center;" | SS ||"[[Inbrief]]" †
||[[Janine K. Spendlove]]
|| 10/11/2015
|- class="short"
||Between [[2 ABY]] and [[4 DBY]]<ref name="Kindling">"The Kindling" features the [[Alliance to Restore the Republic|Rebel Alliance]], which formed two [[Standard year|years]] before the [[Battle of Yavin]] according to ''[[Star Wars: On the Front Lines]]'', and became the [[New Republic]] in [[4 DBY]] according to ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]''. As ''Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico'' also dates the Battle of Yavin to [[0 ABY]], the Rebel Alliance must have been founded in [[2 ABY]] and "The Kindling" takes place some time between these years.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C6D9F0; text-align: center;" | SS ||[[The Kindling]] †
||[[Cavan Scott]]<br />[[George Mann]]

[[2 ABY|2]]&ndash;[[0 ABY]]<ref name="DarkVisions">''[[Star Wars: Vader - Dark Visions]]'' acontece depois da formação da [[Aliança pela Restauração da República]], já que ela aparece nas edições [[Vader - Dark Visions 2|anteriores]] e [[Vader - Dark Visions 4|seguintes]], mas antes da destruição da [[Estrela da Morte]], já que ela aparece nesta edição. ''[[Star Wars: On the Front Lines]]'' data a formação da Aliança Rebelde em [[2 ABY]], e ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]'' data a destruição da Estrela da Morte em [[0 ABY]], o que significa que ''Star Wars: Vader - Dark Visions'' acontece algum tempo antes.</ref>||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | Q ||[[Vader - Dark Visions 2|''Vader - Dark Visions'' 2]] †

|- class="comic"
|[[0 ABY]]<ref name="Obi-Wan mini">{{SW|url=news/marvel-star-wars-may-2022-exclusive-preview|text=A Tale from Obi-Wan's Youngling Days and More from Marvel's May 2022 ''Star Wars'' Comics &ndash; Exclusive Preview}} establishes that ''Obi-Wan'' 1 takes place during [[Obi-Wan Kenobi]]'s final [[Standard day|days]] on [[Tatooine]], and since [[Gender|him]] leaving Tatooine and his [[death]] in {{Filme|IV}} are dated to [[0 ABY]] in ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'', ''Obi-Wan'' 1 must take place around the same [[Standard year|year]].</ref> ||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | Q ||[[Obi-Wan 1|''Obi-Wan'' 1]] †
*<small>Flashbacks ocorrem em [[49 ABY]].</small><ref name="Obi-Wan 1 flashback">The flashbacks in [[Obi-Wan 1|''Obi-Wan'' 1]] take place when [[Obi-Wan Kenobi]] is eight [[Standard year|years]] old, and since {{SWCT|Obi-Wan Kenobi - Padawan - Base Series 1|Obi-Wan Kenobi - Padawan - ''Base Series 1''}} establishes that he was born 57 years before ''Star Wars'': Episode IV ''A New Hope'', which corresponds to [[57 ABY]], he was eight years old in [[49 ABY]].</ref>
||[[Christopher Cantwell]]
|| 04/05/2022
|- class="comic"
|[[0 ABY]]<ref name="Obi-Wan mini" /> ||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | Q ||[[Obi-Wan 2|''Obi-Wan'' 2]] †
* <small>Flashbacks occur between [[44 ABY|44]]-[[32 ABY]].</small><ref name="Obi-Wan 2 flashback">In the [[Obi-Wan 2|''Obi-Wan'' 2]] flashbacks, [[Obi-Wan Kenobi]] is [[Qui-Gon Jinn]]'s [[padawan]]. ''[[Master & Apprentice]]'' establishes that Kenobi became Jinn's padawan when he was thirteen [[Standard year|years]] old. Since [[Star Wars: Card Trader|''Star Wars'': Card Trader]] states he was [[Reproduction|born]] 57 years before the [[Battle of Yavin]]&mdash;[[0 ABY]] according to ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' &mdash;Kenobi became Jinn's padawan in [[44 ABY]]. He remained so until Jinn's [[death]], which occurred in [[32 ABY]] according to ''Galactic Atlas''.</ref>
||[[Christopher Cantwell]]
|| 29/06/2022
|- class="comic"
|[[0 ABY]]<ref name="Obi-Wan mini" /> ||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | Q ||[[Obi-Wan 3|''Obi-Wan'' 3]] †
*<small>Flashbacks ocorrem em [[22 ABY]].</small><ref name="Obi-Wan 3 flashback">The [[Obi-Wan 3|''Obi-Wan'' 3]] flashbacks take place shortly after the [[Defense of Rishi Station]], which appears in "[[Rookies]]." {{TCWcanondates|105}} Therefore ''Obi-Wan'' 3 also takes place around 22 [['ABY-BBY' dating system|BBY]].</ref>
||[[Christopher Cantwell]]

|[[0 ABY]]<ref name="Obi-Wan mini" /> ||style="background-color: #CCC1D9; text-align: center;" | Q ||[[Obi-Wan 4|''Obi-Wan'' 4]] †
*<small>Flashbacks occur between [[20 ABY|20]]-[[19 ABY]].</small><ref name="Obi-Wan 4 flashback">The flashbacks of [[Obi-Wan 4|''Obi-Wan'' 4]] take place after the [[Devaron massacre]] from "[[Monster]]," which ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' dates to [[20 ABY]], and before the end of the [[Clone Wars]], which ''Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico'' also dates to [[19 ABY]].</ref>

|- class="short"
|data-sort-value=4 |[[4 DBY]]<ref name="TLYB Date">"[[The Light You Bring]]" takes place concurrently to [[Project Starhawk]], which in turn takes place during ''[[Star Wars: Squadrons]]''. The game's main story is set four years after the [[battle at Fostar Haven]], which takes place shortly after [[the Disaster]]. As ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' dates the Disaster to [[0 ABY]], the main story and short story must take place around [[4 DBY]].</ref> ||style="background-color: #C6D9F0; text-align: center;" | SS || ''[[The Light You Bring]]''
|[[Joanna Berry]]
|| 08/10/2020
|- class="short"
|data-sort-value=4 |c. [[4 DBY]]<ref name="CTT Date">"[[Count to Three]]" is set shortly after the [[Battle of Endor]], which ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' places in [[4 DBY]]. Therefore, "Count to Three" takes place around the same time.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C6D9F0; text-align: center;" | SS || ''[[Count to Three]]'' †
|[[Joanna Berry]]

|data-sort-value=5 |[[5 DBY]]<ref name="B2-5ABY">''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary]]'' data a reunião de [[Han Solo]] com um [[Ralsius Paldora|desertor]] do [[Império Galáctico]] no [[Castelo Takodana|castelo de Maz]] para obter informações para ajudar na [[libertação de Kashyyyk]] em 29 [[Ano padrão|anos]] antes do [[Cataclismo de Hosnian]], que ocorre em [[34 DBY]] de acordo com ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]''. Portanto, essa reunião e o conflito que se seguiu ocorrem em [[5 DBY]]. Como a destruição do depósito abandonado de armas ocorreu entre a reunião de Solo e a [[Batalha de Jakku]], que ocorre também em 5 DBY, as Missões 7-9 devem também acontecer neste mesmo ano.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C3D69B; text-align: center;" | J ||''[[Star Wars Battlefront II]]'' Campaign: Mission 7: General Distress

|data-sort-value=5 |[[5 DBY]]<ref name="Victory's Price date">{{Penguin|books/609685/victorys-price-star-wars-by-alexander-freed/9781984820075|Victory's Price (Star Wars)|archivedate=20210218050500}} diz que ''Victory's Price'' começa onze meses depois da [[Batalha de Endor]], batalha que ocorre em [[4 DBY]] de acordo com ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]''. A [[Batalha de Jakku]], que ocorre em [[5 DBY]] de acordo com o mesmo livro, começa um ano e quatro meses depois da Batalha de Endor, de acordo com ''[[Estrelas Perdidas]]''. Além disso, ''[[Before the Awakening]]'' diz que [[Kes Dameron]] e [[Shara Bey]] se mudaram para [[Yavin 4]] cerca de seis meses depois de Endor, e ''Galatic Atlas'' diz que isso ocorreu já em 5 DBY. Portanto, ''Victory's Price'' deve ocorrer em 5 DBY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #8DB3E2; text-align: center;" | R ||''[[Victory's Price]]''

|data-sort-value=5 |During or after [[5 DBY]]<ref name="TreeofLife">"The Tree of Life" takes place after [[Lumpawaroo]] was freed in ''[[Marcas da Guerra: Fim do Império]]''. ''Marcas da Guerra: Fim do Império'' features the [[Battle of Jakku]], which ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' dates to [[5 DBY]]. Therefore, the events of "The Tree of Life" must take place during or after 5 ABY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #C6D9F0; text-align: center;" | SS ||"[[The Tree of Life]]" †

|- class="junior"
|data-sort-value=9 |[[9 DBY]]<ref name="Hunters">''[[Hunters: Battle for the Arena]]'' acontece depois da queda do [[Império Galáctico]], que é datado em [[5 DBY]] de acordo com ''[[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas]]''. Nesta história, [[Rieve]] tem 20 anos, mas um dado flashback, que acontece durante a [[Era Imperial]], ela tem 16. Assim, o romance não pode ocorrer mais de quatro anos depois da queda do Império. Como ele também ocorre depois de [[Aran Tal]] se juntar aos [[Caçadores da Orla Exterior]], que ocorre em [[9 DBY]] de acordo com ''[[Star Wars: Timelines]]'', o livro deve se passar neste mesmo ano.</ref> ||style="background-color: #FAC08F; text-align: center;" | RIJ ||''[[Hunters: Battle for the Arena]]'' †

|data-sort-value=25 |[[25 DBY]]<ref name="Scorched">''[[The Star Wars Book]]'' establishes that events of the novel ''[[Bloodline]]'' occur 28 [[Standard year|years]] after those of the film {{Filme|IV}}, which ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' dates to the year [[0 DBY]]; therefore, ''Bloodline'' takes place in [[28 DBY]]. In ''Bloodline'', [[Greer Sonnel]] states that she received her [[bloodburn]] diagnosis three years prior, and the short story "[[Scorched]]" is set when Sonnel is symptomatic but not yet diagnosed; this places "Scorched" in [[25 DBY]].</ref> ||style="background-color: #C6D9F0; text-align: center;" | SS ||"[[Scorched]]"

|data-sort-value=34|[[34 DBY]]<ref name="TPW Date">The [[Del Rey]] ''[[Star Wars]]'' timeline places "The Perfect Weapon" in between [[Canto Bight (novella collection)|''Canto Bight'']] and {{Filme|VII}}. {{SW|url=news/4-reasons-canto-bight-is-an-essential-read|text=4 Reasons ''Canto Bight'' Is an Essential Read|archivedate=20200217011936}} states that ''Canto Bight'' takes place a few [[Standard day|days]] prior to {{Filme|VIII}}, which ''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary]]'' places in the same year as the ''Star Wars'': Episode VII ''The Force Awakens''. ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' dates ''Star Wars'': Episode VII ''The Force Awakens'' to [[34 DBY]], meaning that both ''Star Wars'': Episode VIII ''The Last Jedi'', ''Star Wars'': Episode VII ''The Force Awakens'', and ''Canto Bight'' take place in the same year. Because "The Perfect Weapon" takes place in between ''Canto Bight'' and ''Star Wars'': Episode VII ''The Force Awakens'', it must also take place in 34 [[Galactic calendar|ABY]].</ref> ||style="background-color: #C6D9F0; text-align: center;" | SS ||"[[The Perfect Weapon]]" †

|data-sort-value=34 |[[34 DBY]]<ref name="Episode VIII">{{Filme|VIII}} begins immediately after {{Filme|VII}}, which ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' dates to [[34 DBY]]. ''[[The Star Wars Book]]'' dates the events of ''The Last Jedi'' to 34 [[Standard year|years]] after the end of {{Filme|IV}}, which ''Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico'' dates to [[0 DBY]]. Therefore, the film and concurrent stories are set in 34 ABY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #92CDDC; text-align: center;" | F ||{{Filme|VIII}}

|data-sort-value=34 |Between [[34 DBY]] and [[35 DBY]]<ref name="TMA/Breakout date dote">''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary]]'' places the events of "[[Station to Station]]" shortly after the [[Battle of Starkiller Base]], which ''[[Star Wars: Atlas Galáctico]]'' dates to [[34 DBY]]. "[[The Missing Agent]]" and "[[Breakout]]," take place after "Station to Station" and before {{Filme|IX}}. ''Galactic Atlas'' dates the events of {{Filme|VII}} to 34 [['ABY-BBY' dating system|ABY]] and ''The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary'' places the events of {{Filme|IX}} one [[Standard year|year]] later. Therefore, the events of "The Missing Agent" and "Breakout" must take place between 34 ABY and 35 ABY.</ref> ||style="background-color: #B7DDE8; text-align: center;" | TV ||[[The Missing Agent|''Star Wars Resistance'': Temporada 2: Episódio 12: "The Missing Agent"]] †
||[[Brandon Auman]]
